Tang Juwu's Department Plans Three-Way Counter-Offensive 70

Wang Fengge to Be the Commander of the Northern Route, Xu Dasan to Be the Commander of the Southern Route

Tang Will Be the Commander of the Central Route and Will Attack Tonghua with Li Chunrun

｜War Situation Recently Reported by Luan Fazhang, Commander of the Anti-Japanese Army｜

Special Dispatch from Peiping: A source received a report yesterday from Wang Xiaowen, chairman of the Liaoning Eastern Border National Salvation Association, Tonghua North, Liuhe County, issued on the 1st of this month, stating that after the Japanese army launched a general offensive against our Self-Defense Army on the 11th of last month, it attacked in three routes. Our army also met the attack from four sides. Li Chunrun, stationed in Xingjing County, served as the commander-in-chief of the western route, guarding the Fushun Qingyuan defense line. Wang Fengge's department, stationed in Liuhe, served as the commander-in-chief of the northern route, guarding the Shanchengzhen and Panhai Road lines. Tang Juwu personally led his subordinates to guard the upper and lower reaches of Tonghua South, Ji'an Huanren, and the Yalu River. Xu Dasan guarded the area around Songshuzhen, north of Linjiang County, in the upper reaches of the Yalu River. When the Japanese army's general offensive began, the Western Route Army was the first to respond. In the Battle of Shangxiahe, more than 500 Japanese soldiers collapsed one after another. Our army finally held its original defense. From the 15th, the Japanese army on the north and south routes responded to each other and violently rushed into the northern route army, Wang Fengge's department, with 60,000 troops, fought bravely and fought in more than a dozen battles. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. Whenever there was hand-to-hand combat, our Broadsword Team charged into battle, killing countless enemies. The Japanese army was terrified of them. Therefore, as of now, Wang's department still holds its original defense. The Japanese army, which attacked from the border of the southern route of Korea, combined infantry and air force, plus cavalry and artillery, and had a fierce momentum. Our General Commander Tang (Juwu) personally led his subordinates and fought bravely. However, due to the fierce Japanese artillery fire, the cities of Tonghua and Huanren counties have been bombed by Japanese aircraft for several days in a row, and the people have suffered heavy losses. Tang believes that the Japanese army has sophisticated equipment and that it is not easy to fight on the plains. In order to cherish the lives of the people, he ordered the various departments of the southern route to withdraw from the cities of Huanren and Tonghua on the 22nd, and withdrew along the Tonghua Northeast Ermi Xiaoxicha area to the mountains and forests of Jinchuan, Fusong, Changbai, and Antu. The eastern route, Xu Dasan, withdrew from the city of Linjiang County and guarded the area around the Mosquito Gully Ridge and Songshuzhen. This Japanese army's general offensive did not make contact with the eastern route, so it still holds its original defense. At present, the defense line is that Wang Fengge's department is still in its original defense on the northern route, Li Chunrun's department is still on the border of Xingjing, Qingyuan, and Fushun, and another department has gone south to join forces with Deng Tiemei to attack Fenghuangcheng. The headquarters and the direct troops of General Commander Tang are now concentrated in Jinchuan, Mengjiang, Anchang, Changbai, and Fusong counties. Tang convened a military conference in Jinchuan on the 27th of last month, and senior officers of each army rushed to attend. It was decided to launch a counter-offensive after the military deployment was completed. It is planned to attack in three routes. Wang Fengge is still in charge of the northern route and will advance along the Shenhai Road. Xu Dasan is in charge of the southern route and will attack Linjiang and the Korean border from the Mosquito Gully Ridge in Fusong County. Tang Juwu is in charge of the central route and will go out of Jinchuan to coordinate with Li Chunrun's department in Xingjing County to attack Tonghua from the east and west. The headquarters and the National Salvation Association are now located in Mengjiang Bonai and will be moved to Fusong within a few days for command.

Luan Fazhang, Commander of the 5th Route of the Northeastern People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, now occupies Qingyuan, Yitong, Dongfeng, and other places. The headquarters is divided into twelve departments: Staff, Deputy Officer, Manager, Ordnance, Veterinarian, Communication, Intelligence, Secretary, Military Law, Military Doctor, Diplomacy, and Transportation. It also has four committees: Military Commission, Finance Commission, Political Commission, and Local Committee. It governs a total of two armies, six infantry brigades, two cavalry brigades, a pistol guard team, a guard regiment, and a broadsword team, with approximately 15,000 people. Luan's war report arrived in Peiping yesterday, reporting on the recent combat situation. The original text is as follows: "Our 1st Army attacked Dongfeng on September 3rd and came into contact with the puppet state army and police. I personally directed the front line and fought bloody battles for three days, and finally conquered Dongfeng. On the 17th, the 1st and 2nd brigades of the 1st Army, and a cavalry brigade, attacked Qingyuan, destroyed the Shenhai Road, occupied it for one day and night, and then withdrew. On the 29th, the 6th Brigade of the 29th Army and the 3rd Brigade of the 1st Army, and a cavalry brigade, attacked the Eight Trees area in the Kaiyuan border area, killing more than a dozen Japanese soldiers, obtaining 23 rifles, and burning down the Japanese consulate. On October 9th, the 4th and 5th brigades of the 2nd Army fought with more than 500 Japanese soldiers in Egou, on the border of Xifeng. The Japanese army was surrounded by us and fought fiercely for five hours, killing 90 Japanese soldiers, obtaining 73 rifles, 2 machine guns, a submachine gun, and two boxes of bullets. The war situation will continue to be reported later. Luan Fazhang, Commander of the 5th Route of the Northeastern People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, bows."

They finally arrived at Nanyue Station at 6:50 PM that afternoon. Hengshan County Magistrate Chen Te and Hengyang County Magistrate Zhang Hanyi led personnel from various government agencies and public organizations, as well as military units, in a welcoming line. Chiang, He, and other personnel disembarked amidst the cheers of the crowd and switched to sedan chairs to proceed to Zhusheng Temple for rest. That evening, Chiang, He, and other dignitaries stayed at the Sacred Scripture School, while their entourages stayed at Zhusheng Temple. The following morning (the 3rd) at 7:00 AM, Chiang, He, and others went to Zhusheng Temple in Nanyue to hold a solemn Mount Worship ceremony. The ceremony was entirely modeled after the Confucian ritual, with all formalities observed. A Mount Worship address was also read aloud, stating, "Only God holds power, guarding this southern land. Emperor Shun's southern tour marked the flourishing of democracy. The world is for all, and the great path is open. Over four thousand years, the Premier continued the light. I, Zhongzheng, though lacking in talent, bear the burden of the Central Government. Respectfully, together with my colleagues, I tour Hunan. With pure sincerity, I visit the mountain and offer fragrant sacrifices. May the clouds open across the land, and the nation be peaceful and prosperous."

Observers said that this was an unprecedented grand event since the founding of the Republic of China. After the worship, they began touring the mountain, guided by Wang Hanchuan, the director of the Hengyue Administration Bureau. At that time, Chiang and his wife suddenly felt unwell from the cold and the strong mountain winds, so they could not go along. They stayed at the Sacred Scripture School to rest, with Miss He Mei, the daughter of He Jian, staying at the school to accompany them. The remaining Chiang, He, and others ascended the mountain in fifty-five sedan chairs to visit scenic spots such as Nanyue Temple, Fuyan Temple, Nantai Temple, Zhurong Peak, Jinjilin Bridge, Water Curtain Cave, and She Shen Rock. Wang Hanchuan provided explanations about the history and scenery of each location at all times. Monks from various temples lined the sides of the road, greeting them with cupped hands, and the crowds of onlookers were even more enthusiastic. Chiang was in high spirits.

Photographs were taken at each scenic spot visited, and sixteen pine and cypress trees were planted by the temple gate on the mountaintop by Chiang, He Jian, Liu Jianxu, Liu Yinggu, Wang Dongyuan, Li Jue, Chen Guangzhong, and others, with instructions to the monks to take good care of them as a memento. At noon, they had lunch at Shangfeng Temple. After lunch, they toured Laoshan until 7:00 PM in the evening, having visited all the scenic spots on the mountain. That evening, they originally intended to stay overnight at Zhurifeng in order to watch the sunrise the next day at dawn. However, since the sunrise could only be seen in the eighth month of the lunar calendar, and the time had passed, they all went down the mountain by sedan chair and stayed at the Sacred Scripture School again. On this day, there was an unusual event: the clouds on Mount Heng parted. Mount Heng is the premier scenic spot in the south. From its base to its summit, it is over thirty li high, with seventy-two peaks. Beyond the Halfway Pavilion, it is usually enveloped in mist and clouds, with the scenery obscured. The mountaintop never has a clear day throughout the year. It is said that when Tang Dynasty scholar Han Yu (Changli) and Qing Dynasty Grand Coordinator Wu Rongguang visited, the clouds and mist parted, a tale that has been passed down to this day and recorded in the Nanyue Zhi. Qing Dynasty Zhao Gongyi (Shenqiao) once wanted to see the scenery, but the clouds did not part, so he wrote a couplet to express his disappointment: "Over a thousand years ago, when the Minister of Works toured, who could continue the Poet Sage's resonance? Looking at the seventy-two peaks, since Duke Wen's departure, the mountain clouds have not lightly parted." This story is well known to the people of Hunan. This time, when Chiang visited, the weather was clear and bright, the clouds parted, and the scenery was fully visible. Furthermore, after descending the mountain, it rained that very evening. The general consensus was that this was not only a spectacle but also a truly extraordinary event. After descending the mountain, Chiang, because the Lion Rock in the mountains was a famous scenic spot with many visitors, specially donated 1,000 yuan to Wang Hanchuan to build a stone pavilion as a place for visitors to rest. He also donated 1,000 yuan to Wang Hanchuan to be distributed to the temples on the mountain as a reward. Wang Hanchuan also presented Chiang with a copy of the Nanyue Zhi, a rubbing of the Five Hundred Arhats, and half a catty of Mount Heng wild tea. With this, the mountain tour was complete. Chiang and others had originally planned to return to the provincial capital by car on the 4th, but officials and gentry from Hengshan and Hengyang counties earnestly requested him to inspect the counties. Chiang then took a car with He Jian and others from Nanyue to Hengshan County on the 4th at 11:00 AM for an inspection. It was decided that they would go to Hengyang for inspection on the 5th and review the 15th Division of Wang Dongyuan's troops, preparing to return to the provincial capital on the 6th. Chen Cheng, Li Zonghuang, and others who had traveled to the mountains returned to the provincial capital by car on the 4th and then took an express train to Hankou at 4:00 PM. (November 5th)

Reorganization of Administrative Regions in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province 72

▲Urging the Four Counties of Shang, Song, and South to Convene a Meeting

▲Each County Will Begin Reorganization After Land Survey

The Ministry of the Interior previously promulgated an outline for the reorganization of county administrative regions, which the Jiangsu Provincial Government instructed the Civil Affairs Department to forward to the counties for implementation. Subsequently, Fengxian County reported that Taiping and other townships under the jurisdiction of Nanhui County, and Yexie and other towns under the jurisdiction of Songjiang County, were intertwined with the county, making administrative facilities inconvenient. They proposed to annex them for the purpose of reorganization. Nanhui also submitted a request to annex Chenhang Township under the jurisdiction of Shanghai County for the same reason, while strongly objecting to Fengxian's request. At the same time, Songjiang County also strongly opposed the annexation of its jurisdictions. As a result, this case was endlessly contested and involved the reorganization of the administrative regions of the four counties. They were then separately ordered to convene a meeting of the four counties in accordance with Article 6 of the outline to negotiate a reorganization plan for submission and transfer for approval. However, due to the outbreak of the Shanghai War, it was suspended. It is now being urged to proceed. After it is received, it will be reviewed and reported. Although other county administrative regions have not been reported, it is still difficult to avoid the situation of irregular boundaries. The province is now carrying out land surveys. Actively underway, it is planned to start reorganization after the completion of land measurement and the drawing of detailed maps throughout the province.

Songjiang 73

Tax Police Training Institute, Fourth Term Recruitment: The Tax Police Officer Training Institute of the Salt Affairs Inspection Department of the Ministry of Finance, since its establishment, the first and second terms of students have successively graduated and been assigned to work in salt affairs agencies in various provinces. Robbery at Maojia Bridge, Fengjing: Fengjing has always been a bandit-ridden area. Recently, the paddy fields have just matured, and bandits in the four villages are again planning to make trouble, being very active at the junction of Qingpu and Songjiang. At Maojia Bridge, Sixty-fourth Ward, the house of Yu Guiqing was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits on the evening of the 4th. Each of them had painted faces and carried various types of guns. They broke into the house and first went to Yu Yu'a'lai's room, searching and looting at will, and dragged A'lai off the bed, intending to kidnap him. A'lai escaped naked. His father, Guiqing, heard that the bandits were trying to kidnap his beloved son. Without regard for his own safety, he ran outside and shouted for the capture of the bandits. Immediately, the neighbors gathered and rang gongs to sound the alarm. The bandits fled in panic, firing a shot as they left, wounding Yu Guiqing's leg. The bullet had pierced through. Fortunately, his life was not in danger.

Kunshan 74

Gambler Drowns While Escaping: At Wu Jing Village, about two li from Zhengyi Town in the county, a gambling gathering took place at Wang Xiaoniang's house on the evening of the 6th. This was detected by Wei Xiaohong, the chief of the local public security sub-bureau, who immediately dispatched police to arrest them. Five gamblers were captured and taken to the bureau. On the way, two of them escaped. On the morning of the 7th, a corpse was suddenly found in the river there. It was Wang Lazi, one of the gamblers who had been arrested the night before. Upon hearing this, the villagers were outraged and went to the public security sub-bureau in a group to argue. The order was greatly disturbed. Later, the district office sent personnel to mediate and disperse them. Today (the 8th), the county government sent personnel to the countryside to examine the corpse before further investigation.

Wuxi 75

Dispute Over Road Repairs on the Xicheng Road: The road surface on the northern section of the Xicheng Highway has been severely damaged, making travel difficult. After repeated disputes, the Xicheng Automobile Company raised 36,000 yuan to repair it and pave it with stone slabs. Work began last month and is scheduled to be completed by the end of the year. A road toll collection point has been established to collect fees. During this road repair period, local business cars in Wuxi are not allowed to pass. However, various car companies requested the Jiangyin County Government to reverse its decision, as it affects their business. County Magistrate Ma approved the request, but on the 5th, the Jiangyin County Government suddenly ordered them to stop driving or the cars would be detained. The car owners panicked after receiving the order and went to Jiangyin to petition, stating that if they were hindering the work, they would rather stop driving together with the large car company. The authorities had no choice but to allow them to drive, but with restrictions. The cars resumed normal operation yesterday.

Jiangsu Province Regulates Food Distribution Regionally: The Jiangsu Province food regulation issue was initiated by the Shanghai Municipal Local Association. Meetings were held in Shanghai, Wuxi, and Zhenjiang, deciding that relevant local governments should organize the Jiangsu-Shanghai Food Regulation Association. Regarding the opening of the rice ban in Jiangsu Province, the initial circulation of rice and the prohibition of government and police interference, a telegram has already been sent to the Provincial Government, and the Ministry of Finance and Industry has been instructed to handle it as soon as possible. The representatives petitioned Finance Minister Song, who expressed three points: (1) Free circulation within the country can be followed. (2) Tax collection on imported foreign rice will be implemented after explaining the misunderstanding to the authorities in Guangdong via telegram. (3) The loan of American wheat and the tax on imported goods should still be considered, as the government borrowed only 400,000 tons this year, while the amount of commercial loans in previous years was over 700,000 or 800,000 tons. This year's agricultural products, including wheat, are not surplus, so there seems to be no impact. Afterwards, the association drafted implementation measures. The committee also decided on the establishment of public warehouses. The third group includes nine counties: Wuxian, Kunshan, Changshu, Wujiang, Wujin, Wuxi, Tianyin, Yixing, and Liyang, and it was decided that the chambers of commerce of Wuxian and Wuxi will convene a meeting to discuss together. Wuxi has already scheduled to invite the chambers of commerce and representatives of local relevant organizations from Wujin, Jiangyin, Yixing, and Liyang on the afternoon of the 11th to hold a meeting in Wuxi to discuss the plan. It is also reported that when representatives from each county met in Shanghai, the banking community agreed to provide practical assistance, as it concerns the relief of rural areas. The Bank of China and the Bank of Communications in Wuxi have agreed to lend 200,000 yuan (including Jiangyin) to be handled by the Wuxi Farmers Bank, and the interest rates will be handled in accordance with the Farmers Bank's agricultural lending regulations. Regarding the foreign rice currently stored in Shanghai, there are still 1.4 million piculs. As Tianjin and Guangdong are currently short of rice, Minister Song has telegraphed the financial bureaus of Tianjin and Guangdong to investigate and prepare to transport it by China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ships to facilitate circulation.

Freight Ship Robbed Between Changzhou and Wuxi: The Changzhou-Wuxi ferry of the Xie Xing Shipping Company, which departed from Changzhou to Wuxi the day before yesterday, was passing near the Li Da Petroleum Company several dozen paces from Wuqiao when a vessel suddenly approached, with five strong men ordering it to stop. They then boarded and searched the ship, looting goods and silver belonging to the passengers, resulting in heavy losses. Afterwards, ship owner Qian Desheng reported to the Fifth Public Security Bureau requesting an investigation.

Provincial Government Appoints County Education Directors 84

Selected by the County Magistrate from qualified candidates, not limited to residents of the county.

Nanjing Dispatch, November 8: The Ministry of Education sent a letter to the provincial governments, stating that if the county organization law has been implemented in your province regarding the appointment of county education directors, it should be handled in accordance with the county organization law, with the county magistrate selecting from qualified candidates and requesting the provincial government to appoint them. Efforts should be made to regulate the presence of more or fewer qualified candidates in each county and not be limited to local residents.

Ministry of Education's Interpretation of the Regulations on Pension and Bereavement Payments for Vocational Education Personnel 85

According to Wu Zefan, the principal of Fuzhou Normal School, Article 16 of the Regulations on Pension and Bereavement Payments for Vocational Education Personnel states that if a person receiving a pension dies before two years, half of the bereavement payment stipulated in Article 8 shall be paid. Furthermore, Article 6 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Regulations on Pension and Bereavement Payments states that the pension for vocational education personnel shall be issued by the competent educational administrative agency in four installments in March, June, September, and December. If a vocational education staff applies for retirement in accordance with the regulations and is approved to receive a pension, but dies before the period of issuance, the person has not actually received the benefit of the pension. Can the application for bereavement payment be handled separately, like the situation of vocational education personnel in service and those receiving pensions under Article 16? Also, if a vocational education staff applies for retirement and is approved by the school to receive a pension and a certificate is issued, but the paperwork is delayed, and the person dies before receiving the pension certificate, at the time of death, the person and their family believe they are still in service, but they have been approved to retire. Can the bereavement payment be handled as if they were vocational education personnel in service? The Ministry of Education's interpretation is as follows: If a vocational education staff in a school applies for retirement in accordance with the regulations and is approved to receive a pension, but dies before the period of issuance, or is approved to receive a pension certificate but dies because the paperwork is delayed, it should still be handled in accordance with Article 16 of the Regulations on Pension and Bereavement Payments for Vocational Education Personnel. In addition to the pension they are entitled to, they can also apply for bereavement payments in accordance with the regulations in that article. This is hereby notified.

Settlement of the Teachers' Strike at Liuhe Elementary School 88

Last month, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education dispatched Provincial Inspector Cao Shutian to Liuhe for inspection. Considering the necessity of replacing some educational administrators and principals, the situation was reported to the department. Zhou, the Commissioner of Education, then ordered the county to replace Inspector Sun and dismiss Dong Yanxi, Principal Shi Lin, and others from Liufeng Elementary School. A strict deadline was imposed on the Education Bureau director for all school principals and heads of educational institutions to complete handover and settlement procedures within ten days of receiving the document, with severe consequences for non-compliance. After receiving the document, a meeting of teachers and staff of all schools resolved to both attack the education authorities and strike for salaries. Upon hearing the news, County Magistrate Chen Bingbo summoned all the principals to the county government late at night on the 25th for talks, repeatedly advising them. On the 26th, the schools still went on strike. County Magistrate Chen again gave a speech at the Education Hall in the afternoon to all teachers and staff in the urban area, but to no avail. Consequently, the county government, in accordance with the department's order, detained Gu Ruiyi and two others who incited the student unrest. Yesterday, all schools resumed classes, and those who were detained were released on bail separately.

Local News

Active Efforts by Private Schools in the French Concession to Seek Subsidies 89

Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committee of the Private School Federation

Negotiations with He Zhusun: Not Difficult to Achieve

The Federation of Private Primary and Secondary Schools in the French Concession of this city held its first joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members yesterday at the Huadong Middle School, the federation's headquarters. The executive committee members present were Ma Jiazhen (Huadong), Hong Guang (Guanghua), Shao Peng (Tongyi), Wu Jingbo (Xingzhong), Mao Zhaorong (Nanshang), Wu Yixin (Lehua), Shen Xi (Chongshi), Ou Gesu (Huiping); the supervisory committee members were Song Cheng (Xiangmei), Gong Yiyi (Tianhua), Fu Hai (Dunren), Mao De (Anshun), Wang Dingcheng (Dehua). Chairman Ma Jiazhen presided over the meeting. After formal procedures, the chairman delivered a report (omitted). The following matters were then discussed: (1) Proposal to elect standing committee members of the executive committee. Resolution: Huadong, Nango, and Minguang were elected as standing committee members of the executive committee. (2) Proposal to elect standing committee members of the supervisory committee. Resolution: Dehua was elected as a standing committee member of the supervisory committee. (3) How should the work of the executive committee be allocated? Resolution: General affairs to be handled by the standing committee concurrently, Secretariat by Huiping, Publicity by Chenxi, Organization by Lehua, Accounting by Chongshi, Investigation by Xingzhong and Tongyi. (4) Proposal to appoint members to draft the detailed rules for the executive and supervisory committees. Resolution: To appoint standing committee members to draft the rules. (5) Proposal to appoint members to draft a declaration for developing Chinese education and requesting subsidies from the French Municipal Council. Resolution: Chongshi and Dehua to jointly draft the declaration with the standing committee. (6) Proposal to hold a reception for the press. Resolution: To hold a reception next Monday at 6:00 PM at the Xiyang Western Restaurant. (7) Proposal to petition the Chinese directors and request assistance from the Chinese Taxpayers Association. Resolution: The standing committee to be responsible for this matter. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Interview with He Zhusun: Yesterday, a reporter from the Shanghai News Agency specifically interviewed He Zhusun, Chairman of the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the French Concession, regarding this matter, and the following conversation took place: (Question) What is your association's position on the case of private primary and secondary schools in the French Concession requesting subsidies from the French Municipal Council? (Answer) Our association has not yet received any official documents on this matter, but we are aware of the details through news reports. Once we receive the official documents, we will forward them according to the situation and do our best to assist. (Question) What is the total amount of taxes paid by Chinese residents in the French Concession each year? Is the French Municipal Council neglecting the educational undertakings of Chinese residents? (Answer) The French Concession collects approximately five to six million in revenue each year, of which one-third is paid by Chinese residents and one-third by Westerners. As for the French authorities' efforts in Chinese education, there is only one Chinese Public School that opened this semester. Given the large population of the French Concession, this single school in a remote location is hardly enough to popularize education. (Question) According to your estimation, what will be the outcome of this matter? (Answer) In my opinion, if the schools are determined to implement this and cite the precedent of the Public Concession, and if the Chinese directors demand this based on the rights and obligations of taxpayers, and consistently advocate for this, it should not be difficult to achieve.

Regulations on Subsidies for Chinese Private Schools in the Public Concession 90

Article 10, Section 2 Cannot Be Deleted

Letter from the Public Works Department to the Municipal Education Bureau:

Regarding the request from the Municipal Education Bureau to the Public Works Department of the Public Concession to delete Article 10, Section 2 of the Regulations on Subsidies for Chinese Private Schools established in the Public Concession, it has been learned that the Director-General of the Public Works Department, Mr. Si, cannot express public opinion on this request. Therefore, a letter was sent yesterday in reply to the Municipal Education Bureau with explanations. The original letter from the Public Works Department is excerpted below:

Respectfully, In our reply to the letter from former Director Xu on August 24, regarding the request from your bureau to delete Article 10, Section 2 of the Regulations on Subsidies for Chinese Private Schools established by Chinese residents, our department has carefully considered and reiterated the matter. The important meaning is further elaborated below:

In Article 10, Section 1 of the general regulations, our department has already explained in detail that any private school applying for educational subsidies must be registered with the Ministry of Education or your bureau, and our department will be happy to provide subsidies. The remaining articles in Article 10 mostly treat foreign schools equally. However, Section 2 stipulates that if any school is found to be engaged in anti-foreign activities or is likely to create national animosity, our department will not provide subsidies or will suspend subsidies. This restriction applies equally to both Chinese and foreign schools.

Our department's regulations are entirely for the purpose of maintaining Sino-foreign harmony and preventing adverse effects. Our department will certainly provide assistance. We hope that your bureau understands the responsibility our department bears and cannot agree to the deletion of Article 10, Section 2. This is a further notification for your information.

Director-General Jones.

Free Talk

Random Notes

The Robbery of "Greater China" 107

— Zhan Lu

This is a strange topic that needs explanation.

The robbery (騎刦) is not referring to the Yan general Qi Jie from the Warring States period; it means that pirates mixed into a steamship, and at a signal, they began to act, forcefully ordering the captain to obey the commands of the pirates and sail to a remote location for robbery. Seizing the ship to commit robbery is called robbery (行刦).

"Greater China" is not our Republic of China; it refers to a steamship owned by a Hong Kong company, sailing to Saigon. It was robbed by pirates midway, which happened last month, and the case is still unsolved. The Hong Kong and Guangdong newspapers have detailed accounts.

It is not surprising that ships encounter robbery; what is surprising is that the steamship is called "Greater China," and the pirates who robbed "Greater China" were well-organized. With a single gunshot, they occupied the entire ship, and all the captain, chief mate, and all crew members were under the control of the pirates! Poor "Greater China"! It suffered a terrible disaster in that non-resistance.

After the pirates succeeded, they ordered the captain to change direction, and to avoid being detected by passing ships, they forced the crew to smear a layer of black oil on the yellow smokestack and paint over the three yellow characters "Greater China" on the side of the ship. However, the English name was carved and could not be painted over, so they had to find a way to cover it up. It can be seen that thieves have their own cunning; where did they learn such sneaky, false organizations? It is laughable, and yet lamentable!

Poor "Greater China" was in the hands of the pirates for as long as two days! Only after the robbery was complete did the pirates leave, and "Greater China" was able to safely return. Although the losses were considerable, at least the ship was not taken away, which was a piece of good fortune in the misfortune of "Greater China."

It is alright for "Greater China" to encounter a temporary robbery; it would be terrible if "Greater China" encountered a permanent robbery! It is alright for the three characters "Greater China" to be painted over with black oil for a short time; it would be terrible if the three characters "Greater China" were painted over with black oil for a long time! Speaking of the "Greater China" that had an accident in Nanyang, one cannot help but think of the "Greater China" that had an accident for a long time. Not only was the original name erased, but a false sign was also hung up! Alas! This is a further step!

The Contradictory Life 108

— Tian Fang

｜Contradictions Everywhere｜

My old friend Mr. Cheng, used to be my colleague at a certain news agency, but I haven't seen him for quite some time. Yesterday, he surprised me with a visit, and I learned that he is now working as an inspector at the postal censorship office. I asked him why he left the news industry, and he said that he hadn't actually changed careers, but was simply taking on a side job because his income wasn't enough. I was extremely surprised, because on the one hand, he held a certain position in the press, advocating for freedom of speech, while on the other hand, he was engaging in something without legal basis – because the word "censorship" is not mentioned in the current highest law, the Provisional Constitution – and was actually infringing upon the freedom of speech granted to the people by the Provisional Constitution during the period of political tutelage – Article 15 of the Provisional Constitution – wasn't that strange? So I asked him how these two contradictory aspects of his life could coexist. He shook his head and sighed, saying, "Don't even ask. In the 20th century, isn't everything full of contradictions? People say 'disarmament' but secretly engage in 'military expansion'. The people are starving and freezing, while on the other hand, rice, wheat, and cotton are being dumped and burned. When people attack us with guns and cannons, we chant spells to repel the enemy. The volunteers in the Northeast, lacking food and clothing, fight in the freezing cold, while people in China are spending millions of dollars on a competition. Rickshaw pullers, wearing thin clothes and barefoot, run through the wind and snow, shouting that they're hot, while those riding in the rickshaws, wearing fox fur coats, say they're cold. And so on..." I said, "Enough, enough, you don't need to complain anymore. This is truly a contradictory society. But if there's a problem, it needs to be treated. We have to find a way out!" He said, "Indeed, on the one hand, I'm speaking out for the people and fighting for freedom of speech, but on the other hand, I'm holding back newspapers that contain my own writing. It's all a bit ridiculous. But my life is slipping by in this crack. Sometimes I'm confused, it seems as if I am not really alive. I've even thought about quitting, but what other way out is there? Isn't the world full of contradictions everywhere?"

"Ah, a contradictory life, a contradictory world!" I said with melancholy.

How to Cure Our Forgetfulness 109

— Weng

丨The Impression Given by a Complete History of Resistance Against Japan丨

French General Foch once said, "The greatest crisis for a nation lies in the forgetfulness of its people!" How much of the pain and humiliation we suffered at the hands of the enemy in the spring remains in the minds of most citizens in Shanghai today? Have the bright lights, the intoxicating songs, and the constant dances erased the impressions of the roaring cannons and the heroic blood? This is a question about our national forgetfulness that truly cannot be ignored.

Recently, the Wenhua Company published a "Complete History of the Bloody Battle of Shanghai Against the Japanese," which contains a very detailed collection of images and texts about the bloody battle of January 28th. After flipping through it, not only did it bring back the various passionate and stirring impressions of the time, as if I were reliving an old dream, but even the sounds of the anti-Japanese soldiers charging and the cries of the compatriots on the battlefield seemed to come alive from the pictures, one after another! As a result, my steady breathing became rapid, and my blood, which had gradually calmed down, began to boil again!

Forgetfulness is psychological, not physiological. I dare to say that this "Complete History of the Bloody Battle of Shanghai Against the Japanese" can be considered the only good remedy for forgetfulness. If we hope to eradicate the root of the disease, then this book should not only be read temporarily and occasionally, but also has permanent value to be placed on the desk! (Move remuneration to help the Northeast Volunteer Army)

On Boasting 110

— Cheng Luding

丨Some Thoughts Inspired by Liang Zuoyou’s Work丨

Singing the "Great Advancement Treasure Map," staging the "Empty City Stratagem," this so-called King of Boasting, Liang Zuoyou, came with excitement, left in disappointment, and returned home defeated. The truth is now clear. With some feelings in his heart, he wrote this essay on boasting, and when he has time, he will write another chapter on flattery.

Boasting, boasting! This is enough to represent the thinking of the average Shanghainese, and it can also be said to be a common phenomenon among Chinese people!

I can see many ambitious people who boast, and I can also see many heroes who boast, but I still cannot believe that they have any real power. Exaggerated words and false claims can indeed dazzle people, and at the time, for a moment, they may even receive considerable admiration!

But: a brand that has no branches can hardly adapt to stores like Daoxiangcun and Lugaojian. How can a paper tiger withstand the howling of jackals, and how can a paper cage endure the ravages of wind and rain? Even if a person has vanity and a tendency to exaggerate, which is common, I do not believe that boasting can save the country or benefit anything.

Using people who boast to save the country will only make the country more hopeless, and using people who boast to handle affairs will only make things more unmanageable. If you say that people who boast have any use at all, that's just nonsense. At the same time, people who boast are also the most superficial and trivial.

In fact, things that can be seen with the eyes don't need to be seen by oneself, and mirrors that can reflect people don't need to reflect oneself. So, how can a cow boast about itself? Therefore, this is where Liang Zuoyou failed, and this is also a lesson for many friends who boast.

Funeral Extravagance 111

— Sun Wenni

丨A Study of Filial Sons and Virtuous Grandchildren丨

When people unfortunately break something they love, of course, they are momentarily stunned and reluctant to throw it away. This is indeed the result of love: a surge of regret.

Parents are indeed the most intimate objects of innate love and affection in humanity. If, unfortunately, a death occurs, it is certainly worthy of grief and mourning. But to express the sadness in one's heart, is there no other way besides using extravagant memorial banners, grand funerals, and ostentatious displays? One should also think about whether one's filial piety during their lifetime was sufficient, whether one served them with respect, and fulfilled their ambitions and desires. If you feel that there are one or two areas where you were not able to be thorough, then is this moment of extravagance meant to show off for the dead, or to embellish one's own shortcomings and save face?

Ask: "The deceased finds peace in the earth," what does this mean! If you think it's right, then just find a piece of high ground that is not susceptible to wind and water erosion, bury the remains of the deceased, so that there is no worry of exposure after many years and months, or the disease of being overturned and disturbed. Isn't that also a way to show love for one's parents?

Then again, is the current social trend able to allow people to do this? This is indeed a big question. But the wealthy, in order to blindly follow the trend, spare no expense in wasting money, without considering the wishes of their parents, to create some public welfare. The guilt they deserve goes without saying. And even poor families are not afraid to borrow money to save face. What does this mean?

Brief News: "Lectures on Examples of Translation," written by Wei Rongshuo, a famous English writer and chief writer for the Shanghai Yinghua Lapel newspaper, was published at the end of last month. We were honored to receive a copy from the newspaper yesterday. The content is very detailed and wonderful, divided into three parts: 1) General Translation Examples, 2) News Translation Examples, and 3) News Compilation Lectures. The selection of materials focuses on practical application and is very interesting. The entire book is printed on woodfree paper and priced at five jiao per copy. The newspaper is offering a special deal for English students: a one-year subscription, including one copy of the lectures, costs only one yuan and four jiao, plus five fen for postage. The address of the newspaper is No. 8 Dalianfang, Dalianwan Road, Shanghai.

The Crossroads of Death (9) 112

— Lane Yanqiao

He didn't appreciate how good the twenty-dollar meal was, he only felt that this gathering was more exciting than the wedding feast when he took a concubine the year before. Why should they rigidly separate men and women, with the women's table tucked away deep in the women's hall? After all, since the National Revolution, society has become a little more vibrant.

He returned with a slight buzz from the evening breeze and the glaring electric lights, revisiting the things that had just happened in his lonely bedroom.

He thought that although he had a beautiful wife and concubines at home, "comparisons must be made to distinguish the superior from the inferior." This principle was unavoidable. His first wife was naturally outdated, not worth mentioning. The concubine was still in her prime, and since she had been able to transform from a country bumpkin into a mistress, why couldn't he make her more modern? No, even if her appearance was modernized, her innate, uncarved qualities could not be further sculpted. Unable to read a single word, how could she understand miniature golf or Charleston? She was used to hearing only 18th-century language at home, how could she keep up with the witty and clever remarks that could serve as a modern girl's quotations? No, definitely no, he was discouraged.

Later, he thought, I have plenty of money, why not get another one here? Not as a concubine, but as a girlfriend, that's it! Girlfriends are great, let's pursue one, he became excited again.

Discouragement and excitement fought each other, keeping him awake all night. The next day, he went to his department, and a sense of disappointment arose again.

The female colleague, cursed by the tabloids as a flower vase, handled official business with light and lively movements, and sent it over. Although the characters were written a bit crooked, the fragrance of perfume covered it up, so it didn't seem childish. Although the sentences were a bit difficult to understand, her sharp and crisp words explained them clearly. It would be best if she often brought official business over, deliberately scrutinizing the official business more closely, so that he would have the opportunity to talk to her. When there was no official business for a long time, he would go over to see them work. Thinking of "flower vase," he couldn't help but secretly praise the tabloid's metaphor, the mockery was pleasing. Fortunately, this kind of spiritual comfort made the monotonous political life not so depressing. Too bad the eight-hour workday was too short.

Flour Forward Market Declines 126

Flour Exchange Notice Changes from Using "Metamorphosis" to Using Current Certificates

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month saw a good image again. Imported wheat quotations were better by three or four jiao, and high-quality wheat was better by seven or eight jiao. The exchange also announced that all future buying and selling, whether from factories or customers, must use current certificates. Except for shares in the exchange that can be used as substitutes, all other factory and warehouse receipts and valuable securities will no longer be allowed as substitutes. This restriction did not maintain the momentum of flour prices. Large factories also intended to only bring in and not sell out. Therefore, after the opening quotation, people's hearts were quite shaken, and the opening quotations for each month were one or two fen higher than the previous day, and transactions were quite active. However, after a period of excitement, it gradually subsided, and market prices became weak again. Although the exchange and factories are worried about maintaining prices, the environment is such that they cannot resist it. For example, although Tianjin has daily sales of around 40,000, imported flour already accounts for half of it. Nearly 20,000 bags of Australian flour have recently arrived, and there are still over 500,000 bags being shipped in January, February, and March. Since it was set at 1 tael 2 jiao 6 qian, it can now be cheaper again. Fuxin also dumped over 400,000 in February and March, with prices ranging from 1 tael 8 qian 6 fen to 1 tael 8 qian (delivered in Tianjin). Recently, other companies also wanted to dump it, but there were no buyers. Therefore, if Shanghai flour does not follow the trend, it will be completely monopolized by imported flour. If we do not consider maintaining it, how can we improve it later? In the afternoon, each market was still not good due to foreign countries, and the customers' minds were also unusually weak. Tianjin and Fuzhou both had returns (Australian wheat at 3 taels 4 qian 8 fen, factories only eat at 3 taels 4 qian 5 fen). Small and medium-sized factories also dumped, even though the exchange restricted substitutions. According to the decline in global commodity prices, if this port wants to resist it by force, I am afraid that it will be like a praying mantis trying to stop a chariot, and there will be a yellow bird following behind it. As a result, this month was unchanged, December fell by five li, January fell by one and a half fen, February fell by one fen two and a half li, March fell by one and a half fen, and April fell by one fen two and a half li.

Metals: Pure Antimony Prices Rise Sharply 134

The metal trade was very peaceful yesterday. Although Dongdi customers needed to handle some goods, the number was not large. The transactions on this street were also very ordinary. Therefore, the various markets were very stable. Unfortunately, the price of pure Hunan antimony rose sharply yesterday. Face-to-face transactions were more numerous than before. The price per ton rose from 240 taels to 255 taels. It was said that there were a total of fifty to sixty tons offered for sale. However, the number of goods arriving in later batches was very small, so the price is likely to continue to rise.

Refined Tin Market Gradually Improves 135

The refined tin market has recently been in excellent condition because there are few customers arriving and the demand from various groups is urgent. The price is also expected to gradually improve. Currently, Xiaochong is estimated at 93 taels, Holland at 103 taels, sheet tin at 100 taels, Jianghua at 100 taels, Hengdi at 96 taels, and Yun tin at 82-83 taels.

Pig Lead Market: Externally Strong, Internally Weak 136

The pig lead market has recently experienced strong demand for actual delivery, but the abundant arrival of goods has made people nervous. Therefore, the price has an appearance of being externally strong but internally weak. However, the supply to Guangdong is minimal, so the prospects for the standard product have been declining. Currently, foreign lead is estimated at 12 taels 1 qian and a half, and domestic lead at 11 taels 7 qian and a half. It is heard that apart from occasional transactions in Tianjin, Yantai, and this garrison, there are very limited transactions from other groups. Moreover, overseas pricing has been declining for days, so the market in this port is unlikely to turn around for a while.

Coal: Coal Briquette Market Prices Change 137

Since the issuance of coal briquettes, there have been many categories and the market prices are also inconsistent. Yesterday, the prices of the China Coal Briquette Department suddenly decreased, and the wholesale prices of the same industry in the market also changed accordingly. The wholesale price of old brand briquettes is 25 yuan, loose briquettes is 22 yuan, and steam, stove, and iron stove briquettes is 23 yuan.

Huadong Coal Price Drops 138

Huadong bituminous coal, such as the Ma Wang coal bought by Da Sheng, has recently seen sluggish sales, and the goods piled up in each warehouse are like mountains. It is estimated that there are about 20,000 tons in total, so the price has fallen. Yesterday, the market price was reduced by five qian per unit, and the current selling price is six taels five qian.

Piece Goods: Plaid Worsted Wool Becomes Dull Due to Season 139

Plaid worsted wool was scarce in Shanghai and sales were extremely strong, so the market rose sharply, and the selling price steadily increased. Recently, the weather has gradually turned cold in Japan, causing it to become out of season. Therefore, yesterday, the other party's demand suddenly turned dull. The market in the association appeared weak. The Jia Ning Xian Tu, which sold for 2 taels 9 qian net last week, can now deduct a commission of four or five yuan per box.

Local News

Song Ziwen Flew to Beijing Yesterday 159

Zhang Xueliang's Advisor Also Accompanied

Transferred to Hankou to Meet Chiang and Zhang

Song Ziwen, acting president of the Executive Yuan, took a private Sikorsky plane to Beijing at 7 a.m. yesterday, accompanied by Zhang Xueliang's advisor, Donald, and secretary Huang Chun-dao. He will then proceed to Hankou to meet Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang to discuss military and diplomatic issues in North China. Details are recorded below:

Song Flew to Beijing and then to Hankou: Mr. Song, together with Zhang Xueliang's advisor, Donald, Finance Ministry Secretary Huang Chun-dao, and two guards, took a private Sikorsky plane from Hongqiao Airport to Beijing at approximately 7 a.m. yesterday. After attending a meeting of the Executive Yuan, he took the original plane to Hankou at 11 a.m. to meet with Chairman Chiang. According to Mr. Song, it is difficult to determine whether the second loan of American wheat will succeed. Han Fuju in Shandong has already implemented the withdrawal of troops, which will soon be taken over by the Marine Corps. Liu Zhennian's troops will generally be transferred to Hubei to suppress bandits. The Sichuan affair is an internal problem of that province, and it is believed that it can be resolved. Whether to discuss the reorganization of the Fujian Provincial Government at the next meeting of the Executive Yuan has not yet been determined. The statement that the Japanese side's opinions on the Lytton Report have arrived in Shanghai is inaccurate; the government has not yet received this document, and so on.

Chiang, Zhang, and Song to Meet: It is reported that after Mr. Song arrived in Hankou, Zhang Xueliang also flew to Hankou from Ping. Chiang, Zhang, and Song will discuss military, financial, and diplomatic issues in North China, as well as relations with Japan. According to those close to Mr. Song yesterday, the National Government is now focusing all its efforts on dealing with the Northeast issue. After Mr. Song arrives in Hankou, all aspects, including internal and external finance, must be discussed, but diplomacy is the most important, and so on.

Ministry of Railways Construction

Two-Route Terminal Plan 160

Residents of Designated Areas Petition for Relief

Reporters Banqueted Last Night, Representatives Sent to Beijing

Municipal Government Plans to Prioritize Both Construction and People's Livelihood

China Railway Company Inquires and Demands Overdue Payments

The relocation of the Shanghai North Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, the post-war reconstruction of the Zhabei urban area, and the realization of the Greater Shanghai Plan are of great significance. The Ministry of Railways, in conjunction with the Shanghai Municipal Government, has repeatedly discussed and actively planned this. Jiangwan was designated as the passenger terminal, and Zhenru as the intermodal terminal. The Shanghai Municipal Government announced the acquisition of land needed for the two stations. According to a Beijing correspondent of the Xin Sheng News Agency's interview with the Ministry of Railways, the Ministry recently decided that the two projects are extremely complex and cannot be completed in a short period. They have decided to establish a station within the original railway boundary on Song Park Road as a preparation for the relocation of the North Station. Construction is currently underway. At the same time, they plan to start building the intermodal station first to meet urgent needs. However, the construction of the station is closely related to the traffic on the streets and roads of Shanghai. The Ministry of Railways has consulted with the Shanghai Municipal Government several times, hoping that the road and bridge projects can be connected at the same time as the new station is built, so as to promote each other's progress. The Ministry of Railways' plan, the consultation methods with the municipal government by the appointed councillors Xia Guangyu and Chen Yaozu, and the replies regarding the suspension of property transfers in the designated areas and the petitions from merchants to change routes are recorded separately below.

Ministry of Railways Plan The Ministry of Railways has specially established a Two-Route Construction Committee to specialize in planning the development of the new North Station. The current decisions are: Zhenru will be the permanent intermodal station, and Jiangwan Road will be the Shanghai passenger station. The recently announced area south of the Zhenru Railway, originally intended for acquisition, has been reduced by 198 meters. Another 700 mu or so will be added west of Zhongshan Road and north of Jiaotong Road for the construction of car sheds and transfer tracks. The total construction cost is estimated to be 10 million yuan, and the groundbreaking ceremony is scheduled for New Year's Day next year, with construction starting immediately and a completion period of two years. The land circled for the passenger and intermodal stations will be acquired in accordance with the National Land Acquisition Law, and the funds will be issued by the bank on behalf of the government. The architectural design style has not yet been fully determined. Shanghai is China's only commercial port, and the attention of both Chinese and foreigners is focused on it, so efforts should be made to make it solid and beautiful.

Relocation Methods The Ministry of Railways previously sent Xia Guangyu and Chen Yaozu to negotiate all matters with the Shanghai Municipal Government. The record is as follows: Before the completion of the route connecting the intermodal station to the Jiangwan passenger terminal, a track will be temporarily reserved between Song Park Road and Baoshan Road to facilitate the entry of locomotives into the Wusong factory for repairs. In addition, the route from Jiangwan passenger terminal to the Hongjiang Wharf will be measured first, and the detailed construction methods will be determined by both parties when necessary. The Ministry of Railways believes that the following should be decided as the necessary process for the development of the Zhabei urban area: ㈠ Decide to relocate all tracks and buildings of the railway west of Baoshan Road and east of Datong Road. ㈡ The relocation steps are: First, set up a temporary station on Song Park Road to temporarily replace the existing North Station, and clear the section of land west of Baoshan Road and east of Song Park first. Second, after the completion of the Zhenru intermodal station, move the temporary station on Song Park Road and clear the area. ㈢ The Municipal Government will expedite the construction of Song Park Road from Xinjiang Road to Zhongxing Road to facilitate traffic to the temporary station on Song Park Road. The Municipal Government's Public Works Bureau will send personnel to measure the route of Song Park Road within the road boundary with the Railway Bureau, and immediately establish the road boundary to facilitate the Railway Bureau in determining the location of the temporary station. The Municipal Government's Public Works Bureau will plan the road system within the scope of roads west of Baoshan Road and east of Datong Road, and announce it after obtaining the approval of the Ministry of Railways. ㈤ Decide to start construction of the Zhenru intermodal station and the temporary station on Song Park Road at the same time. The Municipal Government will expedite the construction of the extension lines of Ge Road and Xiaoshadu Road, and the Suzhou River Bridge, to connect with Zhongshan Road to facilitate the Zhenru station. ㈦ Decide to build the Jiangwan passenger terminal at an appropriate time. ㈧ The Ministry of Railways will send personnel in advance to measure the connecting lines between the intermodal station, the Jiangwan passenger terminal, and the Hongjiang Wharf, and draw up drawings for approval. ㈨ The Ministry of Railways will be responsible for the cost of building roads and ditches within the road boundary. ㈩ The Municipal Government will be responsible for the construction costs of ditches and bridges outside the road boundary. ㈩㈠ Decide to request the Executive Yuan to approve and order the Ministry of Interior to announce the circled land.

Location and Scope The location of the Shanghai terminal, as decided by the Ministry of Railways, is the section west of Shida Road, north of Nanxiangyin Road, and along the west side of Zhongshan North Road for 6,000 feet, as the location for the passenger connecting station. The section west of Zhongshan Road and east of Zhenbei Road, along the existing railway line for 3,000 feet north and south, is the location for the intermodal station.

Requests from Residents Ye Youcai and Yu Zhongxian, general managers of Huasheng Electric Factory, petitioned for the exchange of land adjacent to Jiaotong Road because the factory was included in the circled area. The Ministry of Railways stated that it intended to allocate the land, which had already been circled, and it was difficult to approve the request. In addition, Hou Xuanqing and Zhang Lingen and other residents of Wangjiajing, Zhangjiazhai, and Jinxiang in Pengpu District and Zhabei Jiaotong Road petitioned for the avoidance of villages. The Ministry of Railways replied that the Zhenru station is north of the railway and in a necessary location for the route, so avoidance is not possible. Shen Wensheng and Li Xianting and other residents of Lijiajiao, Chenjiazhai, and Wangjiazhai petitioned to avoid the more than 200 mu of land in the six villages including Lijiajiao Village in the Ninth and Tenth Sheng Maps of Zhenru. The Ministry of Railways also replied that avoidance was not possible and that all sections would be acquired in accordance with the Land Acquisition Law.

Ministry of Railways Notice Regarding the announcement, it is noted that the Zhenru Intermodal Station is the hub for passenger transport on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines. All arrangements and plans must be as perfect and applicable as possible to reduce the time for shunting and increase the efficiency of transshipment. The Ministry has reconsidered and made a final decision to slightly change the layout plan of the intermodal station to ensure permanence. The land boundary originally intended to be acquired south of the railway has been reduced by 190 feet from the railway side, reducing the land to be acquired by approximately 1,400 mu. Another area of land north of Jiaotong Road and west of Zhongshan Road, with an area of approximately 700 mu, will be added for the construction of various car sheds and transfer tracks. The revised acquisition of land for the station has been reported by the Ministry to the Ministry of Interior for approval, and the Shanghai Municipal Government has been requested to post maps for announcement. The Jinghu Railway Bureau has been ordered to erect stakes along the boundary as the standard. This notice is hereby issued to inform all landowners in the area to be aware of this and await the price offer for the acquisition. This is the notice.

Municipal Government Instructions The Municipal Government issued an order to the Land Bureau yesterday regarding the request of farmers in Zhenru to avoid the land circled by the Ministry of Railways. Regarding the order to comply, the letter No. 1558 (Industrial) from the Nanjing Office of the Ministry of Railways was approved. The Zhenru Intermodal Station layout plan has been slightly changed, and land north of Jiaotong Road and west of Zhongshan Road must be added. Previously, the letter No. 1386 (Industrial) requested your Municipal Government to issue a public notice to temporarily suspend buying and selling transfers. Regarding the area acquired for the intermodal station, the Ministry will draw up revised land use maps and new plans for the 700 mu of land added north of the railway and west of Zhongshan Road within the original boundary intended to be acquired south of the railway, and report them to the Ministry of Interior for approval and announcement. In addition to examining two copies each of the announcement from the Ministry of Interior and the notice from the Ministry of Railways, issuing them to the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus for posting at the acquisition site, and ordering them to immediately erect stakes separately at the red line boundaries drawn in the revised land use map to identify them, three copies of the revised land use map for the area are hereby inspected, and a copy of the announcement from the Ministry of Interior and the notice from the Ministry are hereby copied for your government to check and announce the acquisition in advance. It is also hoped that you will assist the Land Acquisition Office of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Line Construction Committee in handling all acquisition procedures. A corresponding letter is hereby sent to hope that you will check and handle it, and notify the Land Bureau. Please reply as before, etc. Two copies of the revised land use map for the Zhenru Intermodal Station are attached, and copies of each announcement are sent to your office. Examining the case, the transfer of land circled by the Ministry of Railways has caused panic. Municipal councillors from Zhenru and Pengpu districts, farmers such as Shen Wensheng from the Ninth and Tenth Sheng Maps, and farmers such as Hou Xuanqing from Wangjiajing and Zhangjiazhai, and Zhao Chupei and others from Zhao Family Garden have successively petitioned the Ministry to avoid the land, etc. The matter concerns national construction and the livelihoods of farmers. On the one hand, we should assist as much as possible, and on the other hand, we should find ways to alleviate the suffering of the people. We must plan for both in order to proceed without obstacles. Now, as per the previous procedure, in addition to replying and approving, copies of the draft map are hereby copied and enclosed, and each copy is hereby ordered to the Bureau to immediately comply, and jointly with the Ministry of Railways, carefully inspect and clearly determine the scope of acquisition, and consider the people's sentiments, and find ways to reduce the people's panic, to facilitate the process, and report the measures taken at any time. This is the order.

Reception for the Press Last night at 7 o'clock, the Pengpu District Petitioning Group hosted the Shanghai press at the Zhimeilou Restaurant on Fourth Horse Road. More than 30 reporters from various newspapers attended. During the dinner, Hou Xuanqing, a representative of the villagers, stood up and gave a speech, roughly saying that the Ministry of Railways' construction of the intermodal station and circling of civilian land were unrestricted. The area circled so far has reached six or seven thousand mu. The villagers have lived north of Jiaotong Road for generations, and their livelihoods depend entirely on planting flowers, trees, and vegetables. Recently, they have been affected by the Shanghai Incident, and the cattle industry has declined. Just as they were hoping for government relief, the Ministry of Railways suddenly circled all the farmers' fields and houses. The villagers can neither cultivate nor survive. The villagers' villages are all north of Jiaotong Road and can be avoided in terms of geographical situation. Now, the land that should be avoided is being circled, while the land that should not be avoided is being reduced by more than a thousand mu. The villagers are fighting for their lives and will demand to the end. They hope that their colleagues in the press will uphold justice in their commentary and provide assistance. The villagers are grateful and hopeful for food and clothing, etc.

Petition to the Government Yesterday, the petitioning group submitted a document to the National Government and the Executive Yuan, stating that the Ministry of Railways' indiscriminate acquisition of civilian land in the name of building a new intermodal station for the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou lines, or abuse of public power for private gain, is requested to be thoroughly investigated and the scope of the circled area is limited to avoid villages and protect the people's lives and avoid resentment. The Ministry of Railways is building an intermodal terminal in the area west of Zhongshan Road in Zhabei and in the Zhenru Pengpu area. The two Railway Bureaus have repeatedly stated that the maximum amount of civilian land to be acquired is four or five hundred mu, which is sufficient for use. It has been found that the currently surveyed land occupies approximately three or four thousand mu south of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and approximately one thousand mu north of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway. It is difficult to ensure that there is no abuse of the name of the intermodal station and indiscriminate acquisition of civilian land for future profit. Moreover, the villages circled north of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway are more populated, with approximately 500 households and approximately 1,500 houses. Farmers cultivate flowers and trees for their livelihood. Once forced to relocate, the losses are already considerable, and the state of fragmentation is even more evident. The civilian Shi Rui requested the Ministry of Railways to promptly find a way to avoid the land, but the request has not been approved. The people are unable to bear it any longer and will either create a situation where the river overflows or resort to desperate measures. The Executive Yuan has always valued public opinion and should provide relief to those who have survived the disaster. Therefore, we dare to prepare a document to appeal for investigation, limit the Ministry of Railways to find ways to avoid the villages north of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway to alleviate the people's difficulties and avoid resentment. We are in extreme fear and await orders. We respectfully submit this.

Representatives Go to Beijing Last night, the petitioning group first selected eight representatives, Hou Xuanqing, Zhao Youting, Zhao Wenxiu, Zhang Zhongxiang, Tao Wenyuan, Zhao Zuyan, Zhao Chupei, and Zhao Songfeng, to take the document to Beijing by night express to petition the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Railways, demanding the avoidance of villages. British Demand for Overdue Payments The Shanghai branch of the Sino-British Bank suddenly sent a letter to the Ministry of Railways because of the relocation of the North Station to Zhenru, requesting that the truth be announced and demanding overdue payments. The original letter roughly stated that according to reports in various newspapers in Shanghai, your Ministry recently had a new plan to prepare to relocate the North Station to the vicinity of Zhenru, and the cost of this construction is estimated to be more than 10 million yuan, as well as the addition of buildings, warehouses, platforms, the laying of branch tracks, the construction of a new machine factory, and the relocation of the original machines from Wusong to the new factory. We are extremely grateful for this plan, but we hope to be informed of the truth and the source of the funds. Furthermore, we hope that the overdue debt of 12.8 million yuan will be repaid as soon as possible, etc.

Burmese Government Imposes Land Route Raw Silver Import Tax 161

Ministry of Finance Cables to Instruct Consul in Burma to Negotiate Against It

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from the Yunnan Overseas Chinese Anti-British New Tax Support Association, reporting that the raw silver import tax has now been implemented, and the association received the following reply from the Ministry of Finance:

Yunnan Telegram To the esteemed Shanghai Chamber of Commerce: On October 15th, the Burmese government suddenly implemented a new import tax on raw silver via the Yunnan-Burma land route, with a tax rate of seven annas and a half per ounce, equivalent to approximately 46%, and prohibited the import of Chinese currency. It was not until the 17th that the Yunnan government was notified, causing Chinese merchants to suffer great losses in the raw silver trade thousands of miles along the way, and making it impossible for Chinese merchants to pay off their commercial debts to British Burma, which is of particular importance. Yunnan-Burma trade has a long history, and there has never been a written or de facto tax on the transportation of gold and silver or the circulation of currency between the two countries. The British side has suddenly created a new law, breaking the precedent and destroying the commercial relations between the two countries. Moreover, the announcement was made after the implementation, which is not allowed by law. Hundreds of thousands of merchants in Yunnan and Burma are extremely angry and vow to fight to the death. In addition to cabling the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ambassador to the UK to protest and demand cancellation, your esteemed association, as the leader of the national business community, is requested to unanimously support the effort to achieve the cancellation as soon as possible to save overseas Chinese and maintain the national economy. I am waiting anxiously for your order. Yunnan Support Association of Overseas Chinese in Burma Against New British Tax, respectfully, East.

Ministry of Finance Telegram To the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, please forgive my belated reply. I have examined the telegram, and the measures to reduce taxes on the land borders of our country were cancelled by order in 1929. Goods imported and exported on the Burmese border have been taxed at the full rate in accordance with the tariff for several years. It is not convenient to restore the tax reduction system at this time, which is inconsistent with the principle of taxation that should be followed by the land customs. However, the Burmese government's sudden imposition of import taxes on Chinese goods that have never been taxed will certainly have an impact on trade with Burma in the border provinces. The Ministry has already requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to instruct the Consul in Burma to negotiate against it nearby to provide relief. A corresponding telegram is hereby sent for your information. Ministry of Finance Seal.

City Chamber of Commerce Receives Telegram Announcing Cancellation of Production and Sales Tax on Jiangxi Porcelain 162

Replaced by Business Tax of 440,000 Yuan Annually

No More Branch Offices to be Set Up for On-the-Spot Inspections

Porcelain merchants across the country believe that the production and sales tax in Jiangxi is unbearable and have repeatedly petitioned the National Government for relief, requesting it to be abolished. Recently, Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and Wang Yansong, a standing committee member, accompanied porcelain industry representatives to visit President Chiang Kai-shek and Xiong Shihui to personally explain the difficult situation of the porcelain industry. The Jiangxi authorities initially agreed to change to business tax, no longer setting up offices for inspection. The tax amount is 450,000 yuan annually. Porcelain merchants again requested a reduction. According to news from the City Chamber of Commerce, the matter has been resolved and the tax amount will be reduced. The following is the telegram from the porcelain merchant representatives: To Mr. Xiaolai and Mr. Yansong of the City Chamber of Commerce: Thanks to your strong support and the efforts of Committee Member Fan, the porcelain tax matter has been changed to a business tax with an annual amount of 440,000 yuan, which has been approved and resolved. Special thanks. Yan Zheng, respectfully.

Since the outbreak of the Sichuan War, the General Assembly of the Abolish Internal War Grand Alliance has repeatedly telegraphed to dissuade it, and sent separate telegrams to the chambers of commerce in Chengdu and Chongqing to jointly carry out the effort, but with very little effect. Large Number of Japanese Troops Arrive in Shanghai 166

Marines Head to the Yangtze River The Japanese Ministry of the Navy, on the pretext of troop transfer, has dispatched an additional large group of 625 marines, who have been brought to Shanghai by the special service ship "Takasago Maru." They arrived in port at 4 pm on the 7th and landed at the Osaka Wharf in Yangshupu. Among them, 361 were assigned to the Shanghai Marine Corps, 15 were assigned to the First Foreign Legacy Team Headquarters, 9 were assigned to the Third Fleet Headquarters, and the rest were assigned to various places along the Yangtze River, including 13 to the Saga ship, 41 to the 24th Team ship, 35 to the 15th Team ship, 12 to the Atami and Sumida, 23 to the Fushimi, Futami, Kotaka, and Seta, 49 to the Tenryu, 17 to the Katata and Hotsu, 4 to the Toba, and 6 to the Hira. All the naval vessels going to the Yangtze River are scheduled to depart from Shanghai to various places along the Beijing-Hankou Railway tomorrow morning, while those assigned to Shanghai ships include 15 to the Ataka, 20 to the Izumo, and 12 to the Uji.

Japanese Officers Come to Shanghai to Review Merits The Japanese government specially dispatched Lieutenant Colonels Akashiba and Harada of the Army and Navy, accompanied by Secretary Ide of the Order of Merit Bureau, to first investigate in Dong Shao, and then came to Shanghai by ship from Dalian to review the merits of non-armed Japanese people who assisted in the war and plainclothes teams during the 128 Incident. They also visited Jiangwan and Wusong to see the war results. Chairman Yasui of the Administrative Committee has now handed over the names of people with meritorious service in the Shanghai War to the two officers, who took them back to Tokyo on the Nagasaki Maru last night to apply for merit awards.

The Da Mei Evening News stated that the 2nd Battalion of the British Army Argyll and Sutherland Highlanders arrived in Shanghai yesterday (7th) on the transport ship "Neuralia" from Hong Kong. This morning, they disembarked and proceeded along Nanjing Road to the barracks on Great Western Road for garrison. The bottom of the Lincolnshire Regiment is also returning south on the same ship. In addition, Major General Sunderland, commander of the British forces in China, also arrived in Shanghai on the transport ship this time, because he will hand over to the new commander, Major General Pollard, in February next year. He came to Shanghai to bid farewell to his troops.
