Free Talk

Xu Yulan 229

— Fo

Xu Yulan, a female student from Changchun, plotted to assassinate Pu Yi but was arrested after the attempt failed. Pu Yi's lack of brainpower and ambition, willingly serving as a puppet of the Japanese, certainly deserves to be bombed. It is a pity that the plot was poorly executed, leading to failure and capture.

However, upon closer reflection, Pu Yi is a puppet of the Japanese, or to put it more bluntly, a prisoner of the Japanese. Even if the assassination had succeeded, they could have simply chosen another puppet to take his place. Honestly speaking, success or failure is, on the whole, completely irrelevant. Even if it were intended to "kill the dog to show the monkeys," to warn the hordes of foxes and jackals who are traitors, these traitors, having lost all conscience and heart, would certainly not be moved by it. It is necessary to dissect their hearts one by one, wash them clean, or replace them entirely.

If that is the case, wouldn't Xu Yulan and others have sacrificed themselves in vain? No! Absolutely not. Although Xu Yulan's attempt failed, her spirit, her enthusiasm, her loyalty, and her courage cannot be erased. It is evident that not all Chinese people are like those shameless traitors who can be bought with money or enticed with benefits. There are still people with hearts who have not died, like the volunteer soldiers who fight the Japanese in the bitter cold of Manchuria, risking their lives to fight for the survival of our nation. If they could receive support from Xu Yulan and others, echoing each other from afar, it would be enough to boost their morale and strengthen their resolve to kill the enemy.

Women were originally playthings of men, unable to do things for the country, and to go even further, even despised by humanity. But what about Xu Yulan? Not only should the general male traitors feel ashamed of themselves, but also those within the country who bear the responsibility of defending the territory and shouldering the heavy burden of the nation, I wonder what they think of Xu Yulan's plot to assassinate Pu Yi.

Literature and Art

Inscription on "Autumn Outing Landscape Painting" 230

— Yi Ru

The autumn wind came boundless last night, entering the tip of the brush, giving birth to clouds and mist. The imagery flies in this foot-wide painting, mountains and trees all falling before me. The slanting sun faintly illuminates the desolate grass, a flock of geese startled by the cold comes on the ancient road. Leaves, green before, turn red after the frost, embellishing the autumn scene, not yet old. I further suspect that a scenic spot is in the river ahead, where a guest is setting sail, the white seagulls trying to vie with the man for a seat, rising and falling in the waves, how gracefully. How could I not think of Zhang Han and the perch and water shield? How vast is this autumn scenery! The mountain's meaning contains emotion, as if awaiting me, I am ashamed to be at my desk all day, unable to take a trip at will. I can only indulge in appreciating this painting, as if placing myself in the scene, lingering and halting, bringing forth sorrowful winds. Sorrow comes, my interest ends, I raise my sleeves and lean against the railing, gazing remotely at the sky.

Science

Vinegar 231

— Zu Tong

Principle of Vinegar Brewing: Vinegar is a dilute solution of acetic acid in water, usually containing about 4-10% acetic acid. When wine is invaded by acetic acid bacteria, it turns sour. However, these bacteria cannot reproduce in a pure solution of alcohol and must have nitrogenous substances and salts as their nutrients. Therefore, vinegar making starts with fruit wine, malt beer, wine mash, etc., containing about 6-7% alcohol. After acidification, the alcohol is converted to acetic acid, with the following chemical equation:

C2H5OH + O2 ↓ CH3COOH + H2O

Alcohol Acetic Acid

At the same time, other compounds are formed, with acetaldehyde being the most abundant, which is an intermediate product of alcohol oxidation to acetic acid.

C2H5OH + O ↓ CH3CHO + H2O

Acetaldehyde

Large-Scale Vinegar Brewing: Large-scale vinegar making equipment consists of wooden barrels with perforated false bottoms, on which a thick layer of wood chips is spread. The sides of the barrels are perforated to allow air to enter. The wine is added through a funnel on top and falls onto a rotating disk, dividing into wine flowers, which are sprinkled on the thick layer of wood chips. The acetic acid bacteria rapidly multiply on the wood chips, generating heat, which then oxidizes the passing wine into vinegar. The optimum temperature for acetic acid bacteria reproduction is 40-43 degrees. The vinegar must be stored for several days or months to develop a fragrant aroma, and then filtered with sand. The resulting vinegar contains 6% acetic acid and can be diluted. British "Number 24 vinegar" contains 5.5% acid. Even weaker ones are Numbers 22, 20, 18, and 16. Number 16 contains only 4.1% acetic acid. Vinegar made by diluting acetic acid and adding caramel for color is cheap imitation vinegar.

Shanxi Vinegar Brewing Method: Peas and barley are used as the raw materials for the flour, sometimes with red or black beans added to obtain color. Production is most suitable during the summer. The method uses 65 parts barley, 30 parts peas, and 5 parts red or black beans. Grind finely, add the appropriate amount of water—too dry makes it difficult to grow mold, and too wet makes it difficult to form a mold. Mix well and place in a wooden mold.

Press into a cake shape. Take it out and place it on sorghum stalks or wheat straws, arranged in rows on the ground, surrounded by mugwort, and covered with two layers of paper or wheat straws. Seal the windows and doors tightly. After about two or three days, it will generate heat, and white-green spots will appear on the surface, which is called "Shangmei" (growing mold). If it cannot grow mold by the due date, water should be sprinkled on the cake to moisten it, and the windows and doors should still be covered tightly, making sure that it grows mold. After the mold grows, open the windows for ventilation. After three or four hours, close the windows again, and turn it over once or twice a day. After two weeks, the koji (fermented starter) is formed. Place it in the open air to dry. At this time, if the koji is crushed, the inside will appear red-yellow in color. Each cake weighs about two jin.

The raw materials for the vinegar are yellow millet and sorghum, with 60 parts millet and 20 parts sorghum, respectively cooked with water until they become porridge. Mix them into a vat. After it has completely cooled, add 20 parts koji, stir evenly, and cover with grass. Stir it once a day. At first, the porridge is thick; after seven or eight days, it gradually becomes thinner. After one month, the vinegar slurry is formed. Mix in millet chaff, and rub it evenly with water, not too dry and not too wet. If it is too dry, it is easy to dry out; if it is too wet, it is difficult to generate heat. After rubbing evenly, mix it into a vat and cover it with grass, surrounding it with grass. At this time, the temperature in the house should be around 30 degrees. After seven days, the upper layer of the residue in the vat will generate heat, about three inches thick. Use your hands to move it up and down and rub it. After it gradually cools, cover it again. When the heated layer thickens to five inches, use your hands to move it up and down and rub it again. After that, the heated layer gradually deepens every day and is rubbed every day until the heat reaches the bottom of the vat. Then, rub it once a day for more than ten days, and the residue is formed. After the residue is formed, add it into the vat, which has a hole plugged with a reed pipe, and add water to leach it. However, when adding water, be sure to plug the pipe opening for about an hour to prevent mixing. Place the leached vinegar outside, freeze it in winter, discard the ice and keep the liquid, until the vinegar liquid no longer freezes. Then the vinegar gradually thickens. Then, put it in a closed urn and store it for one or two years before eating. The older it is, the better.

Short Story

The Model Couple 232

— Rui Yucheng

One deep autumn evening, a fashionable young woman stood at a gazebo in the park. Tourists had gradually left, and she was still in the gazebo, looking towards the park gate. She muttered to herself:

(Young Woman) Why hasn't he arrived yet? He has never broken an appointment before! Could it be that he has guessed my hidden intention, knowing that I want to break up with him, and is deliberately avoiding me?! Let's go! What's the point of standing here waiting for him like a fool?

As she said this, she was about to walk away when a young man hurried into the park from outside. As soon as the young man entered the park gate, he stopped and looked around, searching. So she called out first:

(Young Woman) Brother Kai, I'm here! I've been waiting for you for a long time!

Hearing this, the young man immediately strode forward, intending to shake her hand, but she refused.

(Young Man) (With a smile) Oh, Sister Mo, are you perhaps blaming me for being late? I've been really busy these past two days. Just now, I was drafting a notice that had to be sent to the newspaper office before six o'clock, so it was delayed for a long time, making my sister wait here. I'm really uneasy! But since my sister is not an outsider, I think she can forgive me!

(Young Woman) (Shaking her head and sighing) There's no need to say a thousand words or ten thousand sentences. In short, we can only have a friendship relationship from now on! I'm asking you here now, just to break off our engagement!

(Young Man) (His face changed immediately) Sister, what are you talking about? You don't have any obstacles, and I haven't changed my mind in the slightest. What exactly is your hidden reason? Please tell me clearly!

(Young Woman) Alas! You should know that my love is only given to two. One is the country, and the other is you. But love for the country is even more important than love for you. I can't let myself love you and not love the country now!

(Young Man) Sister, what are you referring to by saying that?

If it's really the truth, then I will definitely allow you to fulfill your patriotic ambition!

(Young Woman) Do you even need to ask me this? Your father willingly serves as a traitorous merchant, selling goods from the enemy, regardless of the condemnation of the people. The anti-traitor groups warned him in vain, and the Chamber of Commerce persuaded him without effect. These past few days, the students have been mocking me, saying that I'm the daughter-in-law of a traitorous merchant. You think, I can endure them calling me a cat or a dog; but how can I bear it when they say that I have a relationship with a traitor? Alas, Brother Kai, you must forgive my forced difficulty and allow my request so that you can eliminate the pain in my conscience.

(Young Man) (Laughing loudly) So that's it! So that's it!······

(Young Woman) (Angrily) Do you willingly want to divorce me? Have you also been infected by your father? Alas!·····

(Young Man) You don't know yet, I have already broken off relations with my father. The notice I just drafted can be published in the newspapers tomorrow! You love the country, how can I not love the country? I only regret that I don't have a pistol, otherwise, I would have performed the "Righteous Extermination of Kin" story long ago, and shot him dead! Originally, I had long ago made the determination to break away from him, but the economic problem of studying had not been resolved. Now that all the necessary measures have been planned, what else is there to worry about?······

(Young Woman) (Changing from resentment to joy) Oh, Brother Kai, really?········

As she spoke, she nestled into his arms, and he gave her a sweet long kiss: their consciences were filled with an unspeakable joy.

Improved Society Discussion Group

Page 18

A Suggestion to Abolish Conventional Polite Writing by Buddhist 233

Indeed, we Chinese are the most particular about etiquette. Just look at the exchanges in letters, with terms like "at your knee," "before your honorable presence," "your esteemed self," "your blessed health," "your distinguished footsteps," "your illustrious bearing," and so on. They are expressed with the utmost politeness and humility. But in reality, disciples may not understand principles, and friends may not keep their word. At the slightest disagreement, they turn against each other without mercy. At critical junctures involving self-interest, they are fiercely competitive. Reading their usual correspondence, it's as if they are completely different people. What is the reason for this? Perhaps it is the deeply rooted "hypocrisy" of us Chinese.

Speaking of conventional polite writing, such as birthday prefaces, memorial essays, congratulatory poems, funeral couplets, epitaphs, eulogies, biographies, obituary notices, as well as all sorts of ceremonial banners and inscriptions on silver shields, none of them are without utter nonsense and hypocrisy. Clearly, the person has no noteworthy deeds or commendable virtues, yet they are described in extravagant terms, making them seem worthy of tears and songs. Isn't this also the deeply rooted "hypocrisy" of us Chinese?

Originally, eulogistic tomb inscriptions were already prevalent in the Tang Dynasty. However, congratulatory writings for living people have a shorter history. Therefore, Gui Zhuang stated in his birthday preface that such matters are not ancient practices. Yet, flattering the living is already ridiculous, and flattering the dead is even more so. In ancient times, there were only farewell prefaces, which often contained words of encouragement. Nowadays, people only know how to flatter or boast about themselves, which is completely different from the intentions of the ancients.

There is now a type of scholar who specializes in flattering the living and the dead for a living, and they even claim to be very refined. A birthday preface costs one hundred yuan, and a funeral poem thirty yuan. They sell their writing for a living, preferring not to become officials. Perhaps they are former historians, academicians, or remnants of the Qing Dynasty. Think about it: isn't writing a birthday preface saying that someone has "lived a long and fulfilling life"? Isn't writing a funeral poem lamenting that someone is a "sage withered" or has "returned to the celestial palace"? Friends who make a living by sweet-talking must come to offer flattering words whenever they encounter social gatherings. Servants must also say nice things when their masters have celebrations in order to receive rewards. Then, what is the difference between these great literary figures who sell their writing to praise others for financial gain and those who make a living by sweet-talking or serving as maids and servants? In the decoration shop, I saw a name book of great literary figures, tall enough to hide a person, and I thought about how prosperous their business must be, much better than us literary beggars who submit articles.

Speaking of those who receive such meaningless congratulatory writings, they should not take flattery as interesting or ridicule as honor. For the same old congratulatory and commemorative texts, one might as well buy a "Social Handbook" and copy a few articles. Why spend so much money to consult these boring hermetic literary figures? Moreover, if the name does not match the reality, it is very shameful to receive it. However, it is also unnecessary to send such boring and formulaic articles to others. If you are a wealthy person and send someone a piece of venomous writing, they will cherish it as if it were a treasure. If you are an unknown person, no matter how well you write, even if the wealthy person's hall is large, your work will not even have a place to lean against the wall. Therefore, I have a habit of never sending congratulatory writings to others, nor do I want to ask so-called famous literary figures to write a word or an article. If the matter is truly worthy of commemoration, you might as well ask a few close friends who truly understand you to sign their names in a booklet, which can indeed be kept as a souvenir. I wonder what the editor and readers of this column think?

Random Thoughts

Speaking Foreign Languages is Beneficial 234

Foreigners learn the languages and writings of other countries as tools for studying the cultures and academics of those countries. Therefore, we only see them burying their heads in their studies. Only the citizens of Great China learn foreign languages as a means of livelihood. Therefore, we only see them working diligently with their mouths in a beautiful way. Someone said: "The people of semi-colonies cannot become compradores for foreigners in foreign firms if they cannot speak beautiful foreign languages. Of course, they cannot make a fortune from foreign countries, live in foreign houses, and enjoy foreign blessings..."

Speaking foreign languages to make a living is a unique and original iron rice bowl in your esteemed country, setting a new record unprecedented and unsurpassed!

X X X

Modern men and women, whether giving speeches or chatting, love to interject a word or two, or a sentence or two, of foreign languages. Some people say that this is very fashionable. Once, I asked a friend who always likes to interject foreign languages why he does this. He said: "Sometimes it is difficult to express myself in Chinese, sometimes I cannot think of appropriate Chinese words, and sometimes it is faster to think in English..."

If interjecting foreign languages is fashionable and showing off, then it is understandable, because that is his freedom. But if it is true that "Chinese people find it difficult to express themselves in Chinese and think slowly," then I must doubt what the teacher told me on the platform: "A five-thousand-year-old ancient country, the only land of culture." If this history book were in my hands, I would tear it to pieces and ask it why it deceived me! How dare it speak so brazenly without shame?!

Humorous Drama

"A Scene from a Martial Drama" by a Friend 235

In Shanghai, stores with larger scopes are always double-fronted, while those with smaller scopes are single-fronted. Everyone knows this, but no one has ever used "single-fronted" or "double-fronted" to describe people! Except for Mr. C.

My old friend Mr. C is one of the most humorous and sarcastic among my friends. He often finds shortcomings in others to create "nicknames." His colleague Mr. Y has dark skin, so he calls him "Annamite Police Officer." Old Xu likes to dress up, so he calls him "Rabbit"... In short, he fairly creates a nickname for each of you.

Because of his ability to create amusement, he staged the following martial drama, which may be his retribution!

The incident happened the day before yesterday afternoon. The plot is as follows: Many paintings and calligraphy are hanging on the walls of the parlor, with several tables and benches scattered on both sides. Four people are sitting around a square table, busily playing mahjong. On the left is Mr. H, and below Mr. H is Mr. C, who specializes in making fun of others. Mr. H plays very aggressively and is reluctant to let the player below him take any tiles. Mr. C has lost seven or eight yuan and is naturally angry. He wants to find a shortcoming in Mr. H to vent his anger.

It turns out that Mr. H lost sight in one of his eyes when he was young, becoming one-eyed. So Mr. C's opportunity for revenge has come.

"One-Eyed Mr.! Why can't I take any of the tiles you discard?" Mr. C asked Mr. H with a sarcastic face.

"..."

"Why do you call him One-Eyed Mr.?" someone sitting opposite Mr. C interjected.

"Doesn't he have one eye missing? Isn't 'missing eye' spelled 'One-Eyed' Mr.!" After his clear explanation, everyone burst into laughter.

Mr. H blushed, glaring with his one eye.

The sound of mahjong tiles continued for an hour or two. Mr. C still rarely took tiles from his above player Mr. H and was very resentful. He gave Mr. H another nickname—Single-Fronted.

"If 'Single-Fronted' lets me take a '3-wan' on the edge, my '4-7 wan' pure suit would have won long ago!" Mr. C said, smiling at the other two players.

"What a 'Single-Fronted' nickname! It's both unique and appropriate. Haha..."

"Say 'Single-Fronted' again if you dare," Mr. H said, his anger rising.

"I insist on saying 'Single-Fronted,' what are you going to do?" Mr. H threw a punch. Mr. C was not willing to show weakness and immediately stood up and punched back. Then, the two twisted together. At the same time, the sound of disordered footsteps, chairs falling to the ground, and mouths shouting "Come on! Come on!" all mixed together. The other two players had an inescapable duty to mediate between the two sides, but it was still ineffective. After the two of them used force to pull them apart, each finally stopped. As a result, Mr. C's face had several more finger marks, and "Single-Fronted" Mr. H tore a long gown. A scene from a martial drama finally came to an end, and the sound of mahjong tiles also stopped!

Film Special

International News

Japanese War Films 236

— Ling He

Based on "The Recent Stage of Japanese Films" by Gan Yu

Since the "September 18th" and "January 28th" Incidents, Japan has produced many war films. Because "many tragic pieces of information for upholding the interests of the Manchurian Empire were promoted in the newspapers every day" (original wording; same below). "The noble sacrifice of the Three Brave Soldiers with Explosives, the military exploits of the Four Brave Soldiers as Human Pillars, and the feudal samurai-style devotion of Commander Koga, were all enough to shock the hearts of the Japanese people. Therefore, Japanese war films were built on these facts (?)." "Among them, the Manchurian March of the Shochiku Film Company is considered the best."

In this film, there are many "depictions of post-war life." On the other hand, other war films mostly depict the brave Japanese army and the enemy's revolt from beginning to end. This film focuses on the suffering of the Japanese people after the war.

In addition, there is Nikkatsu's "Great Aerial Attack," which, like Hiroshi Shimizu's "Army Great March," aims to provide the audience with historical knowledge and a belief in worshiping heroes, a dry and uninteresting work.

With the Shanghai Incident as its background, there is "Three Brave Soldiers with Explosives." In this film, "there is the appearance of Shanghai just before the war, with many anti-Japanese crowds shouting to defeat the Japanese and Japanese monks suffering tragic murders by the Chinese." "Whether these facts are true, we do not know." However, "they are the reason for Japan's dispatch of troops. As to whether this reason is proper, we cannot say. However, explaining the reason why the war occurred is very important in the structure of the film."

As mentioned above, Japanese war films have completed the task of military and national education. Moreover, with the close guidance of the military, these films can become tools for propaganda and agitation by the Japanese rulers.

Film Reviews

Review of "Blonde Venus" 238

— Yan Nan

Garbo has left us, but we can comfort ourselves with Marlene Dietrich, whose impressions in "The Blue Angel" and "Morocco" were very unsettling.

Today, "Blonde Venus," which is being shown simultaneously at the Grand and Nanking Theatres, gives people a further understanding of her. Marlene is indeed advancing on the path of art. She performs very considerately: she can make the plot even more tense with silence.

The supporting roles are some new characters, all of whom are not bad. The child who plays Dietrich's son, Dickid Moore, is worthy of attention. His innocent and lively performance adds a lot of color to the film and can truly be compared with David Lee.

The director was originally a famous figure in continental Europe. He can use miraculous means to make this film so moving! In many places, he uses indirect and subtle descriptions. The whole film focuses on small details. This brilliance should of course be attributed to him.

The plot could not be more ordinary. If you read the synopsis of this film, you will definitely not believe that such a good film could come from such an ordinary story, but the fact is often not the case.

In addition, I would like to say a few words. At the first show yesterday at the Grand Theatre, only one reel of charcoal drawing was shown first, and then there was a break. After the break, the main feature was shown. When the first reel was finished, there was another two-minute pause, and more than half of the second reel became silent. This is probably because the two theaters are showing it at the same time and are busy. I think it would be better for the two theaters to show the same film at three o'clock and three fifteen, otherwise, this kind of problem will often occur.

Wang Yuanlong Upholds Justice 239

— Ji Zhong

Wang Yuanlong in the film industry is known for his bold and generous nature and his admirable sense of justice. Recently, due to the persuasion of Mr. Logan, he decided to join the United Film Company. Rumor has it that a group of people with no way out are asking him for help morning and night. He should have gone to Hong Kong earlier, but he has been delayed repeatedly because this matter has not been resolved. However, Mr. Logan's urging has come in the form of flying telegrams, so Yuanlong has to leave early.

Zi Luolan Returns to Her Old Profession 240

— Ji Zhong

Ms. Zi Luolan is famous for her graceful dance and clear voice. Since joining the screen, she has had two works, "Silver River Double Star" and "Overseas Cuckoo Soul." Although the results were not very outstanding, they were still welcomed by some. We fully hoped that she would move forward on the path of strength to seek further education. However, before long, she was hired by Mr. Long, a wealthy household in Hong Kong, who hid her in a golden house, causing her to leave her screen career.

Unexpectedly, news came that Ms. Zi and Mr. Long had divorced due to disagreements. Therefore, Zi Luolan decided to make a comeback and return to the film industry. She is now being introduced by a certain gentleman, and it will definitely become a reality in the near future. The company set is still the United Film Company's second production studio.

Wang Hanlun Joins Zhonghua 241

— Ji Zhong

Xi Yang (Naimé) and Xuan (Jinglin) have made comebacks one after another. A group of old-fashioned stars who have stepped down are quite interested in growing their thighs again and returning to their old professions. Therefore, Zhang Zhiyun followed, re-entering Mingxing. However, news came that Wang Hanlun, an old-fashioned female star in the Chinese film industry twelve years ago, will also return to the silver screen.

According to reports, since Wang retired from the silver screen, she has engaged in the emerging business of beauty salons. For several years, groups have invited her, but Wang Hanlun's conditions have always been so harsh that those who came to hire her were discouraged. Now that Wen Zongyao is organizing the Zhonghua Film Industry Company, he is now collecting talents, and Wang Hanlun is also among those recruited. The two sides have been in progress for a long time, and now all the conditions have been understood. The term is one year, and the monthly salary is four hundred foreign dollars.

— Ji Zhong

Ms. Tang Tianxi has been in the film industry for a long time, and her performance art is quite commendable. Moreover, she has an upward heart, and she is constantly thinking about striving for progress. She has gone directly up to support the ambition as the protagonist from an extra.

Wang Yuanlong's younger brother, Cilong, directed films when he was affiliated with the United Film Company, all starring Tianxi. Now that Cilong has left, Ms. has lost her golden time. In Sun Yu's "Volcanic Love Blood," she only played a supporting role that had nothing to do with the overall situation. Looking back at the past, Tang Tianxi has a sense of vicissitudes.

Film Essays

True Stars are Not Afraid of Many People 244

— Chen Dabei

Stars who only believe in the power of heaven and not in their own abilities, stars who call themselves geniuses and despise newcomers, may be right in what they believe. Because they know that they have no ability, those who are called stars by fluke are just accidental fates. Therefore, they openly admit that they have no ability except to rely on heaven for food. The more stars like this, the farther the performing arts on the screen are from brightness. Fortunately, now in the Chinese film industry, only some of the so-called stars think this way, and the Chinese film industry is not completely buried in darkness.

In the future, those who are called "stars" will not be as easy as they are now. Those who enjoy the glory of stars today, if after five years, they still only rely on the power of heaven, still only rely on support, and do not add a little of their own unique skills, thinking of ways to compete and win in the performing arts, I dare say that he will not be embarrassed to be called a star anymore.

A true star with artistic cultivation will never be afraid of too many people. Not only will they not be afraid of many in the young Chinese film industry, but even the old-fashioned film industry in the United States often feels a lack of it! The only reason why the Chinese film industry's progress is slow and why it is laughed at by a group of friends who love to watch imported films is because most of those stars have not had the opportunity to receive artistic cultivation or how to cultivate themselves. And they have already hung up the sign of stars. If the film industry does not stop competing and progressing, the film industry will never dislike too many stars with artistic cultivation.

Film Common Sense

Beauty | Not Necessary for Stars 245

— Ziyin

When people talk about the success of female stars, they always think that beauty is the only factor. In fact, this concept is wrong, and on the contrary, we can even say that beauty is not necessary for a female star. Perhaps some roles require beauty, but beauty alone cannot create success on the screen.

What the camera is looking for is important expressions and a good inner performance. Even if you have a good-looking face, it is equal to a clay sculpture, and there is no use at all. Even in ordinary social interactions, a female friend who is good at expressing herself is most popular with the public, and on the screen, these expressions, in addition to making people feel happy, also have a greater task for the plot. There are many girls who are for their beauty, there are several guarantees, and they come from afar, among these many beautiful women, which director will choose, and how can those stars who are already famous and not very beautiful, such as Garbo, stand out among these many beauties.

This is the importance of expression, just say Garbo, | to be precise, she can't be counted as a beauty, but what she lacks is made up by her talent, so she still wins the love of most audiences.

Anna Sten, the Russian actress who recently joined Hollywood, is in the same situation. If Ms. Stan is placed among a group of professional women, no one will notice her, but on the screen, her sincere performance allows her to occupy a seat among the red stars.

Joan Crawford cannot stand out in the Caimai Conference, but her art makes her more attractive than the average sensual girl wearing a thin bathing suit. Ruth Chaton also had a smooth journey in the film industry because of the magic of her personality.

To say the most ugly old woman, Helen Hayes, she has been good at acting as a notorious old woman all her life. She is really "sea dragon alive". Her success, in addition to her skills in acting, can be said to be unrelated to the word "beauty".

Because of examples in all aspects, we can draw a conclusion that what a star needs is not just beauty.

Local News

About the United Film Company's First Studio 246

The director of the United Film Company's First Studio, Bu Wancang, can be regarded as an outstanding director in the Chinese film industry. In the past, he supported the United Film Company's First Studio alone and produced many valuable films. However, because Lao Bu was singing a one-man show, no matter how hard he worked, the output was always slower than other companies. The United Film Company's authorities were aware of this, and they also wanted to find a new and bright path for Chinese films, so they successively hired Fei Mu and Jiang Qifeng a month ago to co-star in a three-man show with Lao Bu. From then on, the output of the United Film Company's First Studio may be expected to be faster and more.

Reader's Spring and Autumn

Impressions of "Sharp Hell" 247

— Lu Xiqiao

| is one of Elyssa Reith's trilogy |

Undoubtedly, our Elyssa Reith, the female succeeded in a symphony interwoven with laughter and tears, the song is playing her beauty in the same way, giving full play to her fortitude personality, it is a very fragrant and delicious taste! Indeed, the name of this taste is called "Living Hell"!

Elyssa Reith in "Living Hell" made the masses in front of the screen feel infinite threats, threatening them to sympathize with her to the death, even worship her, every move of hers is like people bathing in the warmth of spring, and at the same time making people fall into the coldness of winter snow, ah! I don't feel that she is stretching her graceful expression in front of Camilla, I directly feel that she is teasing her own "life" on the stage of life.

Friends who went to visit her new work "Living Hell" all said that Elyssa Reith is the proud child of the times, and her expression on the screen directly chases the mysterious female Lang Greta Garbo, but we can't forget the director Frank Lau, and the supporting roles Paul Lucas, Luo Lai Xianeng, and Alexander Ke Lai, etc., green tender leaves, set off her bright flowers.

Here, I will crown her. If you have all appreciated her "Yellow License" and "Girl in Room Thirteen" and feel satisfied, then this "Living Hell" is a delicious song in her trilogy.

Foreign Theory Writing

On the Trend of Soviet Films in the Past Fifteen Years (Continued) 248

— Shi Yi

| According to Harry Alan Potamkin's opinion |

Finally, regarding the film "Golden Mountain," I have to discuss it generally here. No matter whether this film is extremely good or the worst, that is not very important. The main thing is that this film will make the Soviet film route even more difficult. Eisenstein said when he was in the United States before returning to the Soviet Union that he doubted whether films could implement the nature of "concrete evidence." He believed that films were best suited to "general statements." These general statements are "relatively easy," just as melodrama is relatively easy, but not better. The better should be more complete. "Golden Mountain" shows that it is a more complete film. In this film, there are all kinds of inner thoughts and social groups, the inner battles and changes of one person. This is not something that happened in 1914 or 1941, but is exactly what is happening now. Now the experience of the proletarian revolution is proving this fact in the dialectical understanding. This kind of film is not sudden, and its own is a result of dialectics. In many Soviet films, we see the development of the plot reaching its peak, and the protagonist's psychological changes, understanding, and opinions cannot avoid being rigid, such as "The End of St. Petersburg," such as "Storm Over Asia" (it was released in Shanghai at the Baixing Theatre, the film name is not a direct translation, it seems to have been changed to something like "National Soul," not only was the film cut, but at the end, a party flag of the Chinese Kuomintang was added, and I heard that the film merchant deceived the review with the name "German production" and started screening after being modified), such as "A Fragment of the Empire," etc. The above three films, especially the first two, the depiction of mass events is mechanically caught in a kind of overpowering development, or it is made into a kind of concentration of individuals separated from the mass meaning. These phenomena are gone in today's Soviet films. (End)
